[30;1m191 | [0m[35m  - This can even be used in docutils, with the new `myst_inventories` config option[0m
[30;1m192 | [0m[35m  - The `myst-inv` CLI makes it easy to find the correct inventory target[0m
[30;1m193 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m194 | [0m[35m:::{tip}[0m
[30;1m195 | [0m[35mIt is advised (although not immediately necessary) to prefix all internal references with `#`.[0m
[30;1m196 | [0m[35mFor example, `[...](my-reference)`, should be changed to `[...](#my-reference)`.[0m
[30;1m197 | [0m[35m:::[0m
